<userid>103778882665918998476</userid><Response>None< /Response><Rate>1<//Rate><Pictures>None<//Pictures>< Time>
1442554627626</Time>
< Review>
Our party decided to try this restaurant on a whim, without any prior research of its ratings, and it actually soured an otherwise festive night of birthday celebrations. The music/karaoke was obnoxiously loud, and made our dining experience extremely unpleasant. Our waiting time was appropriate, but the dishes themselves were unfortunately underwhelming. The wait staff, if any, were so disinterested in refillling any of our drinks, we were left to wait for our empty glasses of ice to melt, in hopes of satisfying what then seemed like a burden--our thirst. Our dishes were carelessly put together, leaving most of the food soggy and unenjoyable. The food that did appear warm proved to be nothing but a rouse, as the food had in fact been burnt and overcooked. As the night progressed, holding onto the smallest inch of hope, I chose instead to rally for this potential underdog of a restaurant. A foolish decision to make as it became clear to me the recompense would never arrive. After much consideration, the bill was truly unjust. For a group of seven, after divvying the total equally, our dishes were estimated at $12 each; a gracious pricing to an overall dining experience honestly valued at about $5 a plate.

I wouldn't be surprised to learn that this restaurant may have at once been a true relic for cordial eating, but that time has surely left them. What appeared to have once been a jovial atmosphere to dine at, may now have nothing but a cold, disinterested environment left to show for.</Review>

<Time>1609041476333</Time><Text>I've been to Hilltop a good amount of times, and I always enjoy. It is for sure a typical movie theater.

The seats are normal but comfortable. The one thing is that if you go at a popular time it'll take closer to 10-15 minutes to get you snack and popcorn. That can be frustrating, but the popcorn is delicious.

If you go here regularly, then I recommend getting the Cinemark Movie Pass. I save a lot with the discount on tickets and popcorn.

Hope you enjoy yourself!</Text>< rating>
